[30;1m254 | [0m[35m<p>The next 4 examples show how Qhull adds a point. The point[0m
[30;1m255 | [0m[35m[0.5,0.5,0.5] is at one corner of the bounding box. Qhull adds a[0m
[30;1m256 | [0m[35mpoint using the beneath-beyond algorithm. First Qhull finds all[0m
[30;1m257 | [0m[35mof the facets that are visible from the point. Qhull will replace[0m
[30;1m258 | [0m[35mthese facets with new facets.</p>[0m

[30;1m665 | [0m[35magain, Qhull increases the joggle by ten-fold and tries again.[0m

[30;1m667 | [0m[35mof the input points. Qhull reports an error after 100 attempts.[0m

[30;1m36 | [0m[35m<p>Qhull uses dimension-free terminology. Qhull builds a[0m
[30;1m37 | [0m[35mpolyhedron in dimension <em>d. </em>A <em>polyhedron</em> is a[0m
[30;1m38 | [0m[35msimplicial complex of faces with geometric information for the[0m
[30;1m39 | [0m[35mtop and bottom-level faces. A (<em>d-1</em>)-face is a <em>facet</em>,[0m
[30;1m40 | [0m[35ma (<em>d-2</em>)-face is a <em>ridge</em>, and a <em>0</em>-face[0m
[30;1m41 | [0m[35mis a <em>vertex</em>. For example in 3-d, a facet is a polygon[0m
[30;1m42 | [0m[35mand a ridge is an edge. A facet is built from a ridge (the <em>base</em>)[0m
